FNV VOLUMETRIC FOG STAGE OWNERSHIP AUDIT

Questions:
1. Which renderer-owned RGB is final and stable for the world camera?
2. Which writers can replace that RGB between world rendering and image space?
3. Is native fog applied per draw, and can one boundary disable it without missing transparent/forward geometry?
4. What is the safe capture point for volumetric-fog color and native-fog replacement state?

Static-analysis limit:
This audits vanilla code and source-derived NVR intervention sites. It cannot prove runtime plugin ownership, exhaustive draw coverage, or DXVK render-target behavior without runtime telemetry.
